menu-item-object-category menu-item-289106 menu-item-depth-2 sub-menu-item\"><a href=\"https://www.supercars.net/blog/category/misc/top-10-lists/\" class=\" menu-link sub-menu-link\"><span>Top 10 Lists</span></a></li></ul></div></li><li id=\"menu-item-289108\" class=\"hidden menu-item menu-item-type-custom menu-item-object-custom menu-item-has-children menu-item-289108 menu-item-depth-1 sub-menu-item\"><a href=\"http://supercars.net\" class=\"menu-link sub-menu-link sf-with-ul\"><span>Type</span></a><div class=\"sub-menu-wrapper\" style=\"display: none; margin-top: 10px;\"><ul class=\"sub-menu\"><li id=\"menu-item-289084\" class=\"menu-item menu-item-type-taxonomy menu-item-object-category menu-item-289084 menu-item-depth-2 sub-menu-item\"><a href=\"https://www.supercars.net/blog/category/type/classic/\" class=\" menu-link sub-menu-link\"><span>Classic</span></a></li><li id=\"menu-item-289085\" class=\"menu-item menu-item-type-taxonomy menu-item-object-category menu-item-289085 menu-item-depth-2 sub-menu-item\"><a href=\"https://www.supercars.net/blog/category/type/concept/\" class=\" menu-link sub-menu-link\"><span>Concept</span></a></li><li id=\"menu-item-289086\" class=\"menu-item menu-item-type-taxonomy menu-item-object-category menu-item-289086 menu-item-depth-2 sub-menu-item\"><a href=\"https://www.supercars.net/blog/category/body-style/convertible/\" class=\" menu-link sub-menu-link\"><span>Convertible<span class=\"menu-description\">An&nbsp;open-air roadster or convertible sports car is the stuff dreams are made of.&nbsp;During a spirited morning drive there is nothing better than a big engine, small car and open top heaven. Convertible sports cars can be small, light and lithe like the Mazda MX-5 or hypercar performance monsters like the 458 Speciale Spyder or Lamborghini Aventador roadster. These days, with hardtop convertibles systems, advanced materials and body&nbsp;rigidity on par with coupes, you can have your open top fun with serious performance too.</span></span></a></li><li id=\"menu-item-289087\" class=\"menu-item menu-item-type-taxonomy menu-item-object-category menu-item-289087 menu-item-depth-2 sub-menu-item\"><a href=\"https://www.supercars.net/blog/category/body-style/coupe/\" class=\" menu-link sub-menu-link\"><span>Coupe<span class=\"menu-description\">A two-door sporty coupe provides for intimate driving environment with clear performance-aimed styling. Performance coupes can be found for a broad range of motoring tastes and budgets, everything from a small Chevrolet Corvette Stingray or the Jaguar F-Type Coupe right up to supercar territory like the Lamborghini Haracan. We’ve found and reviewed the best Sports Coupes&nbsp;to help you find&nbsp;your&nbsp;cool sports car.</span></span></a></li><li id=\"menu-item-289088\" class=\"menu-item menu-item-type-taxonomy menu-item-object-category menu-item-289088 menu-item-depth-2 sub-menu-item\"><a href=\"https://www.supercars.net/blog/category/body-style/electric/\" class=\" menu-link sub-menu-link\"><span>Electric<span class=\"menu-description\">Electric cars are not a fad and they’re getting really interesting every day. While still emerging, the electric sports cars category is starting to turn out some gems. The Tesla S is a beast. The Mercedes-AMG SLS Electric Drive looks sinister and the R8 e-tron and new Porsche Mission E are all-electric sports cars that move the game forward. It is heating up.</span></span></a></li><li id=\"menu-item-289089\" class=\"menu-item menu-item-type-taxonomy menu-item-object-category menu-item-289089 menu-item-depth-2 sub-menu-item\"><a href=\"https://www.supercars.net/blog/category/body-style/estate/\" class=\" menu-link sub-menu-link\"><span>Estate<span class=\"menu-description\">Need the ultimate combination of space and room? Then you need a fast&nbsp;estate car that has hypercar rivaling speed.&nbsp;They don’t exist you say. Well, they do. Think Audi RS6 and E63 Estate and you’re talking about cars that can carry your dog and still have&nbsp;twin-turbocharged V8 engines and over 500hp. You can have excitement and a very&nbsp;spacious car. Fast&nbsp;estate cars deliver a mouth-watering combination of a powerful engine up front with a huge boot out back, making these cars among the best all-rounders money can buy.</span></span></a></li><li id=\"menu-item-289091\" class=\"menu-item menu-item-type-taxonomy menu-item-object-category menu-item-289091 menu-item-depth-2 sub-menu-item\"><a href=\"https://www.supercars.net/blog/category/type/hot-rod/\" class=\" menu-link sub-menu-link\"><span>Hot Rod</span></a></li><li id=\"menu-item-289093\" class=\"menu-item menu-item-type-taxonomy menu-item-object-category menu-item-289093 menu-item-depth-2 sub-menu-item\"><a href=\"https://www.supercars.net/blog/category/body-style/hybrid/\" class=\" menu-link sub-menu-link\"><span>Hybrid<span class=\"menu-description\">Hybrid sports cars are becoming more&nbsp;impressive vehicles every time a new one is announced. Clearly the Tesla S is a sporty car with that ludicrous launch control and instantaneous torque. Today, hybrid, diesel, and electric vehicles that merge “greenness” with “fun-to-drive” come in almost every style, category, size, and price range.&nbsp;Hybrids will no longer be confined to the driveways of Toyota Prius drivers attempting to squeeze the most mileage out of a gallon of fuel, especially when companies like Porsche build the like of the hybrid 918 Spyder and McLaren the insane P1 with it’s electric unit and big twin turbo V8. Good time.</span></span></a></li><li id=\"menu-item-289094\" class=\"menu-item menu-item-type-taxonomy menu-item-object-category menu-item-289094 menu-item-depth-2 sub-menu-item\"><a href=\"https://www.supercars.net/blog/category/body-style/hypercar/\" class=\" menu-link sub-menu-link\"><span>Hypercar<span class=\"menu-description\">What’s the difference between a supercar and a hypercar?&nbsp;For us, the&nbsp;term hypercar basically means the top tier&nbsp;of supercars. The one percenters. All hypercars are supercars, but not all supercars are hypercars. It is really hard for a supercar to qualify as a hypercar.&nbsp;Million-dollar price tags, no compromises, gorgeous&nbsp;design and unparalleled performance that can’t be beat. Almost every aspect of each car is an advancement in car technology and&nbsp;puts hypercars (clearly) into the top spots of automotive world. Hypercars are the stick against which all cars are meant to be measured.</span></span></a></li><li id=\"menu-item-289092\" class=\"menu-item menu-item-type-taxonomy menu-item-object-category menu-item-289092 menu-item-depth-2 sub-menu-item\"><a href=\"https://www.supercars.net/blog/category/type/kit-car/\" class=\" menu-link sub-menu-link\"><span>Kit Car</span></a></li><li id=\"menu-item-289096\" class=\"menu-item menu-item-type-taxonomy menu-item-object-category menu-item-289096 menu-item-depth-2 sub-menu-item\"><a href=\"https://www.supercars.net/blog/category/type/muscle/\" class=\" menu-link sub-menu-link\"><span>Muscle</span></a></li><li id=\"menu-item-289097\" class=\"menu-item menu-item-type-taxonomy menu-item-object-category menu-item-289097 menu-item-depth-2 sub-menu-item\"><a href=\"https://www.supercars.net/blog/category/type/race-cars/\" class=\" menu-link sub-menu-link\"><span>Race Car</span></a></li><li id=\"menu-item-289099\" class=\"menu-item menu-item-type-taxonomy menu-item-object-category menu-item-289099 menu-item-depth-2 sub-menu-item\"><a href=\"https://www.supercars.net/blog/category/body-style/sports-car/\" class=\" menu-link sub-menu-link\"><span>Sports Car<span class=\"menu-description\">According to the Merriam-Webster dictionary, a “sports car (sportscar) is a small, usually two seater, two door automobile designed for spirited performance and nimble handling”. Makes sense, but it is missing something in this day and age where lines have blurred as technology advances and even everyday cars seem sporty. A GTR or Corvette are clearly sports cars, but what about an E63 AMG Mercedes that is heavy, carries the whole family and has a 500+hp engine? Ultimately, ordinary cars are engineered for comfort, fuel economy, passenger space, and cargo space.&nbsp; They’re designed to be “do everything reasonably well” cars. Some may come with sport styling or ‘sport packages’ or even massive engines. But,&nbsp;it’s a token gesture, a nod to the sports car.&nbsp;True sports cars will have minimal cargo space, minimal seating and performance characteristics that drive most of the decision making car companies went through to build it.</span></span></a></li><li id=\"menu-item-289100\" class=\"menu-item menu-item-type-taxonomy menu-item-object-category menu-item-289100 menu-item-depth-2 sub-menu-item\"><a href=\"https://www.supercars.net/blog/category/body-style/sedan/\" class=\" menu-link sub-menu-link\"><span>Sports Sedan<span class=\"menu-description\">A sports sedan is designed to look and feel “sporty”, offering the motorist more connection with the driving experience, while providing the comfort and amenities expected of a luxury vehicle. For drivers (Dads with kids) who want the exhilaration of a sports car but prefer ample rear seat passenger room, sports sedans are a popular choices, with cars like the BMW M3 or AMG C63 on top of most people’s list. With monster&nbsp;engines, firmer suspension systems and more aggressive looks, sport sedans are a great addition to a family garage.</span></span></a></li><li id=\"menu-item-289101\" class=\"menu-item menu-item-type-taxonomy menu-item-object-category menu-item-289101 menu-item-depth-2 sub-menu-item\"><a href=\"https://www.supercars.net/blog/category/body-style/compact-cars/\" class=\" menu-link sub-menu-link\"><span>Sporty Compact Cars<span class=\"menu-description\">Small sports cars are so much fun. Compact and relatively affordable this is how most of us first experience the supercar bug in real life for ourselves. Sporty compact cars&nbsp;like the Mazda MX-5, Mini Cooper,&nbsp;Volkswagen GTI&nbsp;and&nbsp;Subaru WRX ooze real-life thrills, delivering engaging (and sometimes extreme) performance and driving dynamics&nbsp;with&nbsp;nice&nbsp;styling and the ability to make modifications, they are awesome in our eyes.</span></span></a></li><li id=\"menu-item-289102\" class=\"menu-item menu-item-type-taxonomy menu-item-object-category menu-item-289102 menu-item-depth-2 sub-menu-item\"><a href=\"https://www.supercars.net/blog/category/body-style/supercar/\" class=\" menu-link sub-menu-link\"><span>Supercar<span class=\"menu-description\">Supercars are the best of the best in the automotive world.&nbsp;The best&nbsp;performance, technology, design and price. A race-car level of performance is just the first hurdle and not the only qualifier.&nbsp;Today it seems people are quick to apply the supercar moniker to a wide range of cars (the Nissan GT-R and Corvette Z06 are not supercars folks).&nbsp;A car can’t simply be exotic and expensive either, to warrant the supercar title. A Ferrari California is no supercar. Supercars are mystic creatures . They have an air of mystery. “You just know it when you see it” rings very true.</span></span></a></li><li id=\"menu-item-289103\" class=\"menu-item menu-item-type-taxonomy menu-item-object-category menu-item-289103 menu-item-depth-2 sub-menu-item\"><a href=\"https://www.supercars.net/blog/category/body-style/suv/\" class=\" menu-link sub-menu-link\"><span>SUV<span class=\"menu-description\">Most people are surprised when they find out that Sport Utility Vehicles (SUVs) have been around since the&nbsp;1930s. They truly grew in&nbsp;popularity during the mid-1990s. Traditionally, SUVs were built on&nbsp;truck frames, though more recently they are built more like cars. SUVs harnesses utility attributes and powerful engine performance. Luxury and sports car makes are increasingly launching SUVs to their well-heeled clients. Range Rover, Porsche and BMW have been in the SUV game for years. Now, a newer and even sportier supercar makers are getting involved. Bentley and Lamborghini come to mind, both launching SUVs soon.</span></span></a></li></ul></div></li></ul></div></li></ul>\n</nav></div></div></header></div>\n<section class=\"vw-content-area Lists</span></a></li></ul></div></li><li class=\"hidden menu-item menu-item-type-custom menu-item-object-custom menu-item-has-children menu-item-289108 menu-item-depth-1 sub-menu-item\"><a sub-menu-link\"><span>Classic</span></a></li><li class=\"menu-item menu-item-type-taxonomy menu-item-object-category menu-item-289085 menu-item-depth-2 sub-menu-item\"><a href=\"https://www.supercars.net/blog/category/type/concept/\" class=\" menu-link sub-menu-link\"><span>Concept</span></a></li><li class=\"menu-item menu-item-type-taxonomy menu-item-object-category menu-item-289086 menu-item-depth-2 sub-menu-item\"><a href=\"https://www.supercars.net/blog/category/body-style/convertible/\" class=\" menu-link sub-menu-link\"><span>Convertible<span class=\"menu-description\">An&nbsp;open-air roadster or convertible sports car is the stuff dreams are made of.&nbsp;During a spirited morning drive there is nothing better than a big engine, small car and open top heaven. Convertible sports cars can be small, light and lithe like the Mazda MX-5 or hypercar performance monsters like the 458 Speciale Spyder or Lamborghini Aventador roadster. These days, with hardtop convertibles systems, advanced materials and body&nbsp;rigidity on par with coupes, you can have your open top fun with serious performance too.</span></span></a></li><li class=\"menu-item menu-item-type-taxonomy menu-item-object-category menu-item-289087 menu-item-depth-2 sub-menu-item\"><a href=\"https://www.supercars.net/blog/category/body-style/coupe/\" class=\" menu-link sub-menu-link\"><span>Coupe<span class=\"menu-description\">A two-door sporty coupe provides for intimate driving environment with clear performance-aimed styling. Performance coupes can be found for a broad range of motoring tastes and budgets, everything from a small Chevrolet Corvette Stingray or the Jaguar F-Type Coupe right up to supercar territory like the Lamborghini Haracan. We’ve found and reviewed the best Sports Coupes&nbsp;to help you find&nbsp;your&nbsp;cool sports car.</span></span></a></li><li class=\"menu-item menu-item-type-taxonomy menu-item-object-category menu-item-289088 menu-item-depth-2 sub-menu-item\"><a href=\"https://www.supercars.net/blog/category/body-style/electric/\" class=\" menu-link sub-menu-link\"><span>Electric<span class=\"menu-description\">Electric cars are not a fad and they’re getting really interesting every day. While still emerging, the electric sports cars category is starting to turn out some gems. The Tesla S is a beast. The Mercedes-AMG SLS Electric Drive looks sinister and the R8 e-tron and new Porsche Mission E are all-electric sports cars that move the game forward. It is heating up.</span></span></a></li><li class=\"menu-item menu-item-type-taxonomy menu-item-object-category menu-item-289089 menu-item-depth-2 sub-menu-item\"><a href=\"https://www.supercars.net/blog/category/body-style/estate/\" class=\" menu-link sub-menu-link\"><span>Estate<span class=\"menu-description\">Need the ultimate combination of space and room? Then you need a fast&nbsp;estate car that has hypercar rivaling speed.&nbsp;They don’t exist you say. Well, they do. Think Audi RS6 and E63 Estate and you’re talking about cars that can carry your dog and still have&nbsp;twin-turbocharged V8 engines and over 500hp. You can have excitement and a very&nbsp;spacious car. Fast&nbsp;estate cars deliver a mouth-watering combination of a powerful engine up front with a huge boot out back, making these cars among the best all-rounders money can buy.</span></span></a></li><li class=\"menu-item menu-item-type-taxonomy menu-item-object-category menu-item-289091 menu-item-depth-2 sub-menu-item\"><a href=\"https://www.supercars.net/blog/category/type/hot-rod/\" class=\" menu-link sub-menu-link\"><span>Hot Rod</span></a></li><li class=\"menu-item menu-item-type-taxonomy menu-item-object-category menu-item-289093 menu-item-depth-2 sub-menu-item\"><a href=\"https://www.supercars.net/blog/category/body-style/hybrid/\" class=\" menu-link sub-menu-link\"><span>Hybrid<span class=\"menu-description\">Hybrid sports cars are becoming more&nbsp;impressive vehicles every time a new one is announced. Clearly the Tesla S is a sporty car with that ludicrous launch control and instantaneous torque. Today, hybrid, diesel, and electric vehicles that merge “greenness” with “fun-to-drive” come in almost every style, category, size, and price range.&nbsp;Hybrids will no longer be confined to the driveways of Toyota Prius drivers attempting to squeeze the most mileage out of a gallon of fuel, especially when companies like Porsche build the like of the hybrid 918 Spyder and McLaren the insane P1 with it’s electric unit and big twin turbo V8. Good time.</span></span></a></li><li class=\"menu-item menu-item-type-taxonomy menu-item-object-category menu-item-289094 menu-item-depth-2 sub-menu-item\"><a href=\"https://www.supercars.net/blog/category/body-style/hypercar/\" class=\" menu-link sub-menu-link\"><span>Hypercar<span class=\"menu-description\">What’s the difference between a supercar and a hypercar?&nbsp;For us, the&nbsp;term hypercar basically means the top tier&nbsp;of supercars. The one percenters. All hypercars are supercars, but not all supercars are hypercars. It is really hard for a supercar to qualify as a hypercar.&nbsp;Million-dollar price tags, no compromises, gorgeous&nbsp;design and unparalleled performance that can’t be beat. Almost every aspect of each car is an advancement in car technology and&nbsp;puts hypercars (clearly) into the top spots of automotive world. Hypercars are the stick against which all cars are meant to be measured.</span></span></a></li><li class=\"menu-item menu-item-type-taxonomy menu-item-object-category menu-item-289092 menu-item-depth-2 sub-menu-item\"><a href=\"https://www.supercars.net/blog/category/type/kit-car/\" class=\" menu-link sub-menu-link\"><span>Kit Car</span></a></li><li class=\"menu-item menu-item-type-taxonomy menu-item-object-category menu-item-289096 menu-item-depth-2 sub-menu-item\"><a href=\"https://www.supercars.net/blog/category/type/muscle/\" class=\" menu-link sub-menu-link\"><span>Muscle</span></a></li><li class=\"menu-item menu-item-type-taxonomy menu-item-object-category menu-item-289097 menu-item-depth-2 sub-menu-item\"><a href=\"https://www.supercars.net/blog/category/type/race-cars/\" class=\" menu-link sub-menu-link\"><span>Race Car</span></a></li><li class=\"menu-item menu-item-type-taxonomy menu-item-object-category menu-item-289099 menu-item-depth-2 sub-menu-item\"><a href=\"https://www.supercars.net/blog/category/body-style/sports-car/\" class=\" menu-link sub-menu-link\"><span>Sports Car<span class=\"menu-description\">According to the Merriam-Webster dictionary, a “sports car (sportscar) is a small, usually two seater, two door automobile designed for spirited performance and nimble handling”. Makes sense, but it is missing something in this day and age where lines have blurred as technology advances and even everyday cars seem sporty. A GTR or Corvette are clearly sports cars, but what about an E63 AMG Mercedes that is heavy, carries the whole family and has a 500+hp engine? Ultimately, ordinary cars are engineered for comfort, fuel economy, passenger space, and cargo space.&nbsp; They’re designed to be “do everything reasonably well” cars. Some may come with sport styling or ‘sport packages’ or even massive engines. But,&nbsp;it’s a token gesture, a nod to the sports car.&nbsp;True sports cars will have minimal cargo space, minimal seating and performance characteristics that drive most of the decision making car companies went through to build it.</span></span></a></li><li class=\"menu-item menu-item-type-taxonomy menu-item-object-category menu-item-289100 menu-item-depth-2 sub-menu-item\"><a href=\"https://www.supercars.net/blog/category/body-style/sedan/\" class=\" menu-link sub-menu-link\"><span>Sports Sedan<span class=\"menu-description\">A sports sedan is designed to look and feel “sporty”, offering the motorist more connection with the driving experience, while providing the comfort and amenities expected of a luxury vehicle. For drivers (Dads with kids) who want the exhilaration of a sports car but prefer ample rear seat passenger room, sports sedans are a popular choices, with cars like the BMW M3 or AMG C63 on top of most people’s list. With monster&nbsp;engines, firmer suspension systems and more aggressive looks, sport sedans are a great addition to a family garage.</span></span></a></li><li class=\"menu-item menu-item-type-taxonomy menu-item-object-category menu-item-289101 menu-item-depth-2 sub-menu-item\"><a href=\"https://www.supercars.net/blog/category/body-style/compact-cars/\" class=\" menu-link sub-menu-link\"><span>Sporty Compact Cars<span class=\"menu-description\">Small sports cars are so much fun. Compact and relatively affordable this is how most of us first experience the supercar bug in real life for ourselves. Sporty compact cars&nbsp;like the Mazda MX-5, Mini Cooper,&nbsp;Volkswagen GTI&nbsp;and&nbsp;Subaru WRX ooze real-life thrills, delivering engaging (and sometimes extreme) performance and driving dynamics&nbsp;with&nbsp;nice&nbsp;styling and the ability to make modifications, they are awesome in our eyes.</span></span></a></li><li class=\"menu-item menu-item-type-taxonomy menu-item-object-category menu-item-289102 menu-item-depth-2 sub-menu-item\"><a href=\"https://www.supercars.net/blog/category/body-style/supercar/\" class=\" menu-link sub-menu-link\"><span>Supercar<span class=\"menu-description\">Supercars are the best of the best in the automotive world.&nbsp;The best&nbsp;performance, technology, design and price. A race-car level of performance is just the first hurdle and not the only qualifier.&nbsp;Today it seems people are quick to apply the supercar moniker to a wide range of cars (the Nissan GT-R and Corvette Z06 are not supercars folks).&nbsp;A car can’t simply be exotic and expensive either, to warrant the supercar title. A Ferrari California is no supercar. Supercars are mystic creatures . They have an air of mystery. “You just know it when you see it” rings very true.</span></span></a></li><li class=\"menu-item menu-item-type-taxonomy menu-item-object-category menu-item-289103 menu-item-depth-2 sub-menu-item\"><a href=\"https://www.supercars.net/blog/category/body-style/suv/\" class=\" menu-link sub-menu-link\"><span>SUV<span class=\"menu-description\">Most people are surprised when they find out that Sport Utility Vehicles (SUVs) have been around since the&nbsp;1930s. They truly grew in&nbsp;popularity during the mid-1990s. Traditionally, SUVs were built on&nbsp;truck frames, though more recently they are built more like cars. SUVs harnesses utility attributes and powerful engine performance. Luxury and sports car makes are increasingly launching SUVs to their well-heeled clients. Range Rover, Porsche and BMW have been in the SUV game for years. Now, a newer and even sportier supercar makers are getting involved. Bentley and Lamborghini come to mind, both launching SUVs soon.</span></span></a></li></ul></div></li></ul></div></li></ul>\n</nav></div><div class=\"vw-side-panel__sub-menu\" style=\"top:
